  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3d54c964-4afe-4db1-bb02-a3d730554ecc'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

  <span id="freeText18326990348589802668" style="display:none">Abby has been through hell and has survived one of the most brutal childhoods imaginable... barely. <br /><br />To the outside world she is just a loner with an attitude. <br /><br />When her grandmother dies in a tragic explosion, Abby is left with questions-and nothing else. <br /><br />Homeless, sleeping in a junkyard, and on the run from a system that has failed her over and over again, she meets Jake, a tattooed blue-eyed biker with secrets that rival her own. <br /><br />Two broken souls that can't be healed. They can't be saved. <br /><br />Abby &amp; Jake have to decide if they can accept the darkness not only within one another, but within themselves. <br /><br />If they can accept each other for who they really are, they might be able to learn that love isn't always found in the light.<br /><br /><i><b>Caution:</b> This is not your typical romance. The story of Abby &amp; Jake contains disturbing situations, graphic violence, sex, strong language, drug use, and all types of abuse. </i><br /><br />Dark Needs, A Dark Light of Day Novella, is available now.</span>

<div id="review_716297091" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/716297091" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/716297091?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716297091" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3340813665308918365"> ★★★★★ <b>5 Damaged Stars!!!</b> ★★★★★<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a1476e93-68cb-4dea-abdb-c04954122714_zps420359d0.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436176i/881514.jpg' alt='The Dark Light of Day photo a1476e93-68cb-4dea-abdb-c04954122714_zps420359d0.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This was not your average love story. It was beautiful, but broken and intense. Abby and Jake’s journey was not an easy one... this story wasn’t all happy, but I thoroughly enjoyed reading it. The writing was fluid, the plot was unpredictable and I loved how it ended. <br/><br/><br/>Abby Ford has only had one person in her life who she loves, who means anything to her, her Nan. Abby had a terrible and traumatic childhood. The last four years have been the closest to normal sh</span>
  <span id="freeText3340813665308918365" style="display:none"> ★★★★★ <b>5 Damaged Stars!!!</b> ★★★★★<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/a1476e93-68cb-4dea-abdb-c04954122714_zps420359d0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436176i/881514.jpg" alt="The Dark Light of Day photo a1476e93-68cb-4dea-abdb-c04954122714_zps420359d0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was not your average love story. It was beautiful, but broken and intense. Abby and Jake’s journey was not an easy one... this story wasn’t all happy, but I thoroughly enjoyed reading it. The writing was fluid, the plot was unpredictable and I loved how it ended. <br><br><br>Abby Ford has only had one person in her life who she loves, who means anything to her, her Nan. Abby had a terrible and traumatic childhood. The last four years have been the closest to normal she’s ever had. On the night of her high school graduation, her Nan is tragically taken. Abby is left completely alone. No job. No place to live. No means to support herself. She finds herself sleeping in her Nan’s old truck at the junk yard. There she meets Jake Dunn.<br><br>Jake Dunn has spent the last four years away from this town, his father, and all the memories he’s left behind. He is a biker, a loner who doesn’t get attached to anyone. He has too many secrets. Jake has to come home to take care of some business. While at his fathers garage, he sees her. <br><b>
  <blockquote>The night I met Abby Ford, my life changed forever.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/null_zps859b0cea.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436176i/881515.jpg" alt="The Dark Light of Day photo null_zps859b0cea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is something about Jake Dunn. Abby feels safe around Jake. And that is very rare for her. Jake feels the need to protect Abby, to take care of her. He genuinely wants to help her. Abby doesn’t feel worthy of Jake, but he knows that’s just not true.<br><i>
  <blockquote>“You’re not nothing. Don’t ever fucking say that again, because you’re everything.” He said it again, quietly this time, “You’re fucking everything, Bee.” </blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/null_zpsc6974322.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436176i/881516.jpg" alt="The Dark Light of Day photo null_zpsc6974322.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jake makes everything a little better. Abby is worried that if Jake knew about her childhood, her past, the things she can’t do (she has an aversion to people touching her) he wouldn’t want her anymore. What Abby fails to realize is Jake wants all of her. The good, the bad, the broken. Jake's not perfect. He has some major secrets and skeletons of his own that he is equally afraid of Abby finding out. He's terrified that she will want nothing to do with him when he tells her. <br><br>Abby and Jake are both broken in their own ways. Together, they work. I loved the two of them together, their friendship that grew into a relationship. Abby’s past is terrible. Jake’s occupation is controversial. When Jake finds out about Abby's past, he is kind, loving, understanding. Abby takes Jake's job very well. Better than he ever expected. They are both a mess, but together they work.<br><b>
  <blockquote>We were just us, broken and bruised, fucked-up and messy, and together we were everything we never thought we could be.</blockquote>
</b><br>Jake and Abby grow closer. For the first time in her life, Abby is able to open up to someone, to be with someone physically, emotionally, in all ways. She feels connected to Jake. She can share things with him she has never told a soul, she can be physically intimate for the first time ever. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/cd1fc06d-36e2-4481-b003-858d85ed7daa_zps31660cfd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436176i/881517.jpg" alt="The Dark Light of Day photo cd1fc06d-36e2-4481-b003-858d85ed7daa_zps31660cfd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Just as they are getting somewhere in their relationship, Jake has to leave town for a while for a job. If poor Abby hasn’t been through enough already, she goes through something even more traumatic while Jake is gone. It’s devastating. It’s disturbing. It will break your heart. <br><br>Abby is the most brave, strong and resilient heroine. I can’t imagine going through all she went through. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Fresh wounds mixed with old scars. A portrait of my life in pain. Proof that I had been beaten, but I wasn’t broken. <br>They couldn’t fucking break me.</blockquote>
</b> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/null_zpse29c392e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436176i/881518.jpg" alt="The Dark Light of Day photo null_zpse29c392e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So much more happens in this story. Jake and Abby suffer more tragedy than any two people should ever have to bear. It makes you wonder how much destruction and devastation one person can bear. Jake and Abby’s road is rocky. It’s not an easy ride... <br><b>
  <blockquote>We’d almost healed each other once, and the pain of being almost healed is worse than the pain of being broken to begin with. </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Jake and Abby are two characters that couldn’t be farther from perfect, but they are perfectly damaged, perfectly flawed, and above all else- perfect for one another. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/null_zps99c2ac83.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436176i/881519.jpg" alt="The Dark Light of Day photo null_zps99c2ac83.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story was difficult to read at times <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is a pretty graphic rape scene, a long with some terrible memories of child abuse from Abby’s past <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <i>The Dark Light of Day </i> hit all the right buttons for me. A darker storyline, broken characters, a damaged man, tough not annoying heroine, heartbreaking and sad, but heart warming at times... and most importantly, gave me a case of the feels. This one will evoke some strong emotions in you. The Dark Light of Day is about so much more than finding love and healing. It’s about a girl, a girl who endured more than suffering and trauma than any person should ever go through, finding the strength to move on. That it’s okay to be touched, to fall in love, to find happiness and let people in. Jake and Abby were able to find beauty in all the ugly. A fantastic debut novel I would recommend! <br><br><i>**ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review**</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3340813665308918365" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4621838673173256815">After reading King and Tyrant from T.M.Frazier I was very interested in Jake's character. He had a minor role in the King series but he still was the character that I liked the most. So, I was ecstatic to learn that he has a book as well. <br/>And I have to say that I prefer this book to the King series. <br/><br/>I was also very pleasantly surprised by Abby, I did not expect that I would end up liking her and my heart broke for her several times over. And if I liked Jake in King series, I like him more now, e</span>
  <span id="freeText4621838673173256815" style="display:none">After reading King and Tyrant from T.M.Frazier I was very interested in Jake's character. He had a minor role in the King series but he still was the character that I liked the most. So, I was ecstatic to learn that he has a book as well. <br />And I have to say that I prefer this book to the King series. <br /><br />I was also very pleasantly surprised by Abby, I did not expect that I would end up liking her and my heart broke for her several times over. And if I liked Jake in King series, I like him more now, even if he has prime idiot moments. <br />However, while I expected this book to be dark, I did not expect all of what happened to happen.</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer714350787" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5181360657007339743"><b>1 star</b><br/><br/>WARNING: CONTAINS MEGA SPOILERS AND A VERY RANTY CLASS A BITCH WHO CAN'T GET OVER THIS TRAINWRECK-IN-DISGUISE STORY<br/><br/>Aside from the ridiculously high ratings, I chose to read this book for two reasons: a personal request and a blogger friend who repeatedly assured me I would like it based off of my tastes. Too bad that this is what I think:<br/><br/><b>Insta-love makes me vomit.<br/><br/>Pregnancy annoys me (unless the couple is already married or if the author <i>really</i> convinces me).<br/><br/>Inserting unnecessary time gaps </b></span>
  <span id="freeText5181360657007339743" style="display:none"><b>1 star</b><br><br>WARNING: CONTAINS MEGA SPOILERS AND A VERY RANTY CLASS A BITCH WHO CAN'T GET OVER THIS TRAINWRECK-IN-DISGUISE STORY<br><br>Aside from the ridiculously high ratings, I chose to read this book for two reasons: a personal request and a blogger friend who repeatedly assured me I would like it based off of my tastes. Too bad that this is what I think:<br><br><b>Insta-love makes me vomit.<br><br>Pregnancy annoys me (unless the couple is already married or if the author <i>really</i> convinces me).<br><br>Inserting unnecessary time gaps just adds fuel to the fire.<br><br>Illogical sequence of events makes my intellect shrivel.</b><br><br>IMO, this story has all the above and then some. <br><br><u>I struggled with the entire book but here are the main points that made me ask myself: Are these characters fucking stupid?</u><br><br>1. Insta-love: I really loved the prologue and how it set up both Abby and Jake's painful pasts so I could see how broken these two characters are. But when they meet it's literally love at first sight and after 4+ years of staying away from others and emotionally distancing themselves, they open up to each other in a snap! The dude was getting a blowjob from some skank three days ago and he loves Abby in just days?!?! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393017602ra/8648807.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>2. Jake and his profession. If you're a killer, you don't just start spilling your secrets presto. Legit?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393017602ra/8648808.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>NO!!!!!!</b> Plus this part of him isn't really revisited until the very end :/<br><br>3. Abby and her touch dislike. Because of tragic circumstances in her past, Abby avoids any kind of physical contact. But again, in just a matter of days, she's hugging and kissing and almost having sex with Jake. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388065974ra/7731933.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh yes, Amy, really.<br><br>4. What an asshole Jake is: there is nothing redeemable about him. Let me set it up for you: Abby loathes and is terrified of Owen (an ex-friend when he tried to get in her pants). She opens up about her past and tells ALL her secrets to Jake. She trusts Jake, and loves him. Jake knows all this. <br><br>So WHY THE FUCK does Jake assume she went behind his back and slept with Owen when she actually got brutally raped by him?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?!?! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393019684ra/8649055.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393020471ra/8649176.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After all his claims of love, he doesn't TRUST her and has constant jealousy spurts. Good riddance.<br><br>5. What a wimp Abby is: it was Jake's fault for not believing her but it was her fault too for NOT TELLING JAKE WHAT HAPPENED! Oh and did I mention she gets pregnant?????<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380427977ra/855871.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6. Just at the part where I thought I was going to jump off a cliff from how annoying these characters are, the author does something that completely made me go bonkers.<br><br><b>&gt;TIME JUMP!!!!! Let's fast forward to 4 years later!&lt;<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393019004ra/8648976.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WHAT.<br><br>THE.<br><br>FUCK.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393019735ra/8649077.gif" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>7. The 4 years later story. So after 4 years, Jake decides to barge into her life again and wants to take control but is spitting mad when Abby tells him the kid (Georgia) isn't his but actually Owen's (as a result of the rape). He still is pissed that Owen touched her and she still WON'T TELL HIM WHAT REALLY HAPPENED. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393020428ra/8649173.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>8. Who the father actually is. Turns out it's Jake's because you know, the story just <i>has</i> to be perfect. Wouldn't want Owen to blemish anything would we? *insert sarcastic snort* In the 4 years Abby has Georgia, she NEVER even thought about getting a paternity test?!?! I mean she just assumed it was Owen's because of the eyes? Like what the everliving fuck. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/350700.gif" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked the ending but the epilogue ended on a weird note. <br><br><b>Thanks Christine for helping me get through this and listening to me rant at 3 AM!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393020872ra/8649212.gif" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5181360657007339743" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12054585471505898944"> <b>5 DARK CAPTIVATING STARS!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435717i/880458.jpg' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>"I fell asleep that night in the arms of a killer.I'd never slept better."</b><br/><br/><b>"We were just us.Broken and bruised.Fucked up and messy.And together we were everything we never thought we could be."</b><br/><br/>Wow this book definitely become one of my favorites!!It is so intense!! The story of Abbey and Jake is different and captivating!! This book explores a darker side of humanity...it will captivate you!!I couldn't put it down!! <br/><br/> <b>The Dark Light of Day is about Abby's and Jake's life.</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12054585471505898944" style="display:none"> <b>5 DARK CAPTIVATING STARS!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435717i/880458.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>"I fell asleep that night in the arms of a killer.I'd never slept better."</b><br><br><b>"We were just us.Broken and bruised.Fucked up and messy.And together we were everything we never thought we could be."</b><br><br>Wow this book definitely become one of my favorites!!It is so intense!! The story of Abbey and Jake is different and captivating!! This book explores a darker side of humanity...it will captivate you!!I couldn't put it down!! <br><br> <b>The Dark Light of Day is about Abby's and Jake's life...two souls that have lived through hellish childhoods ..</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435717ra/880459.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Abby is 17 year old.. had already been through a lot...her parents abused her... and she had never known what it was like to be hugged or kissed or even loved by anyone... Barely surviving her painful past, and now losing her Nan, the first person to actually care for her.. she starts to give up on life until she meet Jake...who gives her something to live for... <br><br> Jake seems to come into Abby’s life right when she needs him the most....But he has his own problem too..<br><br><b>"We're all a little damaged Bee.Some of us more than others."</b><br><br>his past mold him to become a killer for hire...In Jake, Abby finally found someone who will protect her. For the first time in her life, the person who is supposed to love her doesn't want to hurt and abuse her...<br><br>I loved Jake and Abby's relationship. I loved seeing Jake pushing her over and over to open up, and how he refuses to let her push him away. I loved that how he got close to Abby was by revealing things about himself. The way they got to know each other was beautiful.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435717i/880460.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Abby was so broken and even though she was closed off you could still see that she was strong and didn't take shit from anybody.<br>I loved Jake so much!!He is a badass killer who rides a bike but he loves Abby so much that he would literally do anything for her...and I agree with him in the book no matter how wrong it may be..... .<br><br><br>I absolutely loved this book because it was so different from anything else I have read. I never thought I would fall in love with these characters, but they captured my heart!!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer704001942" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1517242340245290869"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875992.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>4.5 You are a survivor, you are a warrior Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875993.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Abby might only be seventeen years old but she's been through whole lot more than people twice her age. When her Nana dies, she's left alone in the world, homeless, she ends up sleeping in a junkyard. This is when she meets Jake, he's blonde has blue eyes, but he has an inherent darkness surrounding. Abby feels safe around him, and that gut feeling is proven right when he saves her from a situation she swore she would never get back into again.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875994.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875995._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Th</span>
  <span id="freeText1517242340245290869" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875992.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>4.5 You are a survivor, you are a warrior Stars!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875993.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Abby might only be seventeen years old but she's been through whole lot more than people twice her age. When her Nana dies, she's left alone in the world, homeless, she ends up sleeping in a junkyard. This is when she meets Jake, he's blonde has blue eyes, but he has an inherent darkness surrounding. Abby feels safe around him, and that gut feeling is proven right when he saves her from a situation she swore she would never get back into again.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875994.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875995._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then there's Jake, with his good looks and questionable occupation. He quickly realises that he want Abby for himself. But having had an almost as bad break as Abby, he does not feel worthy. But that isn't enough to try and stop him from being part of her life. He becomes her protector, and slowly Abby begins to open up to him. he'd do anything or her, kill anyone for her. All she has to do, is give the go ahead and he won't think twice about it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875996.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They're love isn't a conventional one, but they both begin to heal because of it. But unfortunately not everyone wants to see them find happiness. Because of this they're love is tested in the most harsh and heartbreaking way. Can they're love persevere, will Jake prove himself worthy of Abby's love, and will Abby finally be able to take down the walls she's been using as shield all her life. The only person to break through was her Nana, and now she's gone from her life.<br><br><u>
  <b>My Thoughts</b>
</u><br>This was me while reading this book:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434383ra/875997.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Maybe I'm just a wimp, but dear God the stuff that happened to this girl was too much for my heart to bare! This story is a about pain, suffering and loss, but then the characters also learnt to forgive and let go of the past and live in the now. I thoroughly enjoyed reading it although I was a sobbing mess.<br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by author in return for an honest review!</i><br><br><b>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875998._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/875999._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/876000.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434383i/876001.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Images are courtesy of author's Facebook and Twitter pages</i><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TM-Frazier/126354187462961?fref=ts" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a><br><a href="https://twitter.com/TM_Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718628271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16652156814656369932"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FrazierThedarklightofdayTitebySueBee_zpsc23dbad9.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385283215i/7117099.jpg' alt=' photo FrazierThedarklightofdayTitebySueBee_zpsc23dbad9.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/jax-teller-riding-on-a-motorcycle_zps09a6f7c3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385283215ra/7117100.gif' alt=' photo jax-teller-riding-on-a-motorcycle_zps09a6f7c3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★! The Dark Light of Day (stand-alone). A beautiful tale of survival, endurance & a love that blossoms in spite of adversity!</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Hope had been stripped from me at every minute of every hour of every day for my entire life.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>The Darker Light of Day</b> is a story about <b>17-year old Abby Ford who has had a horrible upbringing</b>. and just learned that the only person who ever loved her, her grandmother, Nan just passed away. <br/><br/><b>Jake Dunn has just returned to town</b>. He left when </span>
  <span id="freeText16652156814656369932" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/FrazierThedarklightofdayTitebySueBee_zpsc23dbad9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385283215i/7117099.jpg" alt=" photo FrazierThedarklightofdayTitebySueBee_zpsc23dbad9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/jax-teller-riding-on-a-motorcycle_zps09a6f7c3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385283215ra/7117100.gif" alt=" photo jax-teller-riding-on-a-motorcycle_zps09a6f7c3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★! The Dark Light of Day (stand-alone). A beautiful tale of survival, endurance &amp; a love that blossoms in spite of adversity!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Hope had been stripped from me at every minute of every hour of every day for my entire life.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The Darker Light of Day</b> is a story about <b>17-year old Abby Ford who has had a horrible upbringing</b>. and just learned that the only person who ever loved her, her grandmother, Nan just passed away. <br><br><b>Jake Dunn has just returned to town</b>. He left when <b>tragedy struck his family in his late teen years</b>. He is now 22 years old and has come home to organize the family business. <br><br>Jake and Abby strike up a <b>friendship of sorts</b> and so their <b>journey begins</b>... The story follows these two broken souls as they <b>deal with their pasts, uncover each other’s secrets and face more unimaginable hardship</b>. <br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/CH1bysb_zpsac255375.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385283215ra/7117101.gif" alt=" photo CH1bysb_zpsac255375.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b><br><a>Jake Francis Dunn: </a>22 years/hit man/dark blond hair/blue eyes/goatee-tattoos.</b>
</i><br><br>Six words to describe <b>Jake: Lost, broken, focused, smart, caring and lonely</b>.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I like the way you make the silence bearable.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20heroine/Blake-Lively-Blowing-Hair_zps0ca6b906.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385283215ra/7117102.gif" alt=" photo Blake-Lively-Blowing-Hair_zps0ca6b906.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b><br><a>Abby Marie Ford: </a>17 years/high school graduate-unemployed/red hair/blue eyes/scars.</b>
</i><br><br>Six words to describe <b>Abby: Resilient, strong, determined, broken, naïve yet wise beyond her years.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I fell asleep that night in the arms of a killer. I’d never slept better.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b> The Darker Light of Day is a beautiful and poignant story!</b> Much befalls Jake and Abby so have a box of tissue handy. I already sympathized with them from the beginning and so at times it felt it was just too much adversity….<br><br><b>Excellent storytelling! Compelling and endearing characters! A journey of endurance and rising above the odds!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“We were looking right into each other. Broken soul to broken soul.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 4 stars <br>Heroine rating: 4 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 3.5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 3.5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 3.5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 4.5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 4 stars<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this book: Probably not.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20hands/tattoo2bysb_zpsf42fedf7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385234917ra/7104495.gif" alt=" photo tattoo2bysb_zpsf42fedf7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC provided to me by author in exchange for an honest review. </i>

<div id="review_765850421" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/765850421" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/765850421?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer765850421" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18312464221777811334"><img width='100%"' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384738931i/6951775._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384547438i/6899800._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br/><br/><b> This book was just... WOAH!! </b> (4.5 stars)<br/><br/>After several readers told me that this was one of the best books they'd read this year, I decided to try out the first chapter just to get a taste of what they were talking about... welp, three hours later it was 4AM and I was sitting there still reading and unable to put it down. It just quietly drew me in and didn't let go.<br/><br/>I <em>love</em> books that can take me by surprise and this was one of them! It was totally unpredictable! I fi</span>
  <span id="freeText18312464221777811334" style="display:none"><img width='100%"' src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384738931i/6951775._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384547438i/6899800._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br><br><b> This book was just... WOAH!! </b> (4.5 stars)<br><br>After several readers told me that this was one of the best books they'd read this year, I decided to try out the first chapter just to get a taste of what they were talking about... welp, three hours later it was 4AM and I was sitting there still reading and unable to put it down. It just quietly drew me in and didn't let go.<br><br>I <em>love</em> books that can take me by surprise and this was one of them! It was totally unpredictable! I find it so refreshing to genuinely feel like the story is taking you for a ride. And what a <em>crazy</em> ride this one was!!<br><br>Dark, gritty, a touch sexy, very brutal and unforgiving at times, but also beautiful and heartwarming... And it had that delicious quiet angsty feeling I love so much where you feel like you just <em>need</em> for things to be okay but you're not quite sure how it's ever going to be able to get there.<br><br>And in the second half, things got <em>intense!! </em>I mean <em>ohhhhh boy!!! </em> The <em>stuff</em> that happens is like one sucker punch after another. I'm not kidding. This book knocks you to the ground and then kicks you when you're down. Over and over again. But... it also picks you back up and helps you heal.<br><br>This was not a fairy tale. This was not a fluffy romance. This was <em>not</em> your "typical" romance. This was a dark, gritty, sometimes twisted, story of two abuse survivors, scarred both inside and out by their pasts who found something in each other that helped them both not only to feel whole again and to heal but also to embrace their darker sides and to learn that "love isn’t always found in the light."<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>
      <em>"We were looking right into each other. Broken soul to broken soul."</em>
    </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>But I'm getting ahead of myself here. First, a little about the book....<br><br>It's been years since Jake went back to the small town he came from. When his last remaining family turned against him, he left and didn't look back and went on to become a professional hitman for hire...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I contributed nothing and took everything. But to be fair about it, I also expected nothing from the godless world that ripped me apart at every turn. I expected nothing, until the night I met a certain redhead with attitude.<br>The night I met Abby Ford, my life changed forever."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>When Abby loses her grandmother in a freak explosion, she is left alone in the world ten months shy of her 18th birthday. Determined not to be thrown back in "the system" that  has failed her over and over again and left her permanently scarred, she runs away and hides out for the night in a junkyard.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I wasn't the happy ending type… I was the fucked-up kid that fucked-up shit happened to. Why had I ever though I deserved more?"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>That's where she meets Jake -- gorgeous, tattooed, with bright blue eyes and deep dark secrets. Their meeting was not a conventional one (ohhh no!) and neither was their relationship, but somehow it worked perfectly for them...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I fell asleep that night in the arms of a killer. I'd never slept better."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I really don't want to say too much more about the plot because it's worth discovering their journey for yourselves. It was an intense, emotional roller coaster. As a result of their respective nightmares, both Abby and Jake had built up such high walls guarding their hearts that it wasn't easy for them to get to know each other.<br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We're all a little damaged, Bee. Some of us more than others."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>There were so many unanswered questions as they tried to figure each other out...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Why do you carry a gun?"</em>
    <br>
    <em>"I've answered this one for you before. Because there are some dangerous people out there."</em>
    <br>
    <em>"Yeah. But you've never said if you were one of them or not."</em>
    <br>
    <em>"What if I am? … Would it matter?"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Abby's walls were especially high. Over and over again, she'd learned the hard, brutal way not to trust anyone so it was very hard for her to let Jake in... but he was persistent. He made her feel safe. And for the first time in her life, she found someone who made her feel worthy of love.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I want to help you. I want to hold you. I want to make it all okay for you. I want to fucking touch you because you're the most beautiful person I've seen, and I can't imagine never being able to hold your hand or kiss you."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Jake was such an interesting guy. He was... hmmm, well, let's just say he wasn't your average hero. His secrets were dark and gritty (just like the book) but also heart breaking, tragic and downright chilling in places. But he had this badass protective side to him that just made me trust him without question. And Abby did too. I think she could sense that this guy would move mountains to keep her safe. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I loved all of him, the good and the bad, the light and the dark."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Abby's past was downright horrific. Gruesome. The very worst of the worst of the worst. The people she'd been subject to were just sick and she'd been left scarred both inside and out, never able to escape the nightmares of her past. When she opened her eyes, she could see them; when she closed her eyes, she could remember them. <br><br>My heart just <em>broke</em> over and over again for both Abby and Jake, but especially for Abby. This girl had been through <em>hell</em>. Literal hell. But she was one tough girl. Despite being utterly screwed over by life again and again and again, she was so resilient and never let anyone push her down for good.<br><br>Now, the first half of the book was good and I couldn't put it down. But HOLY. HELL. The second half just had my heart in my throat!!! It was one shocker after another. Just when I thought it couldn't get worse - BAM!!!! It took me by surprise several times and in places, it was just a steady stream of me sitting there going <em>ohmyGodohmyGodohmyGodohmyGod!! </em>.... <em>INTENSE!!! </em><br><br>Guys, this book is not for the faint of heart. It. does. not. hold. back.<br><br>This might sound weird but the second half kind of had a similar vibe to <i>The Sweet Gum Tree</i> (which is one of my most favorite books, so this is a big compliment) mixed in with shades of Dexter (yup, for real) and almost a smidge of Kristen Ashley-like badass too... I'm trying to explain it here without spoilers which is not easy. And this is just describing the vibe alone, 'cuz the plot itself was really unlike any other I've read.<br><br>Ok now the ending. First thing you should know is that it is a HEA. No cliffhanger, no loose ends, no tragic ending, and no lead-in to a sequel. The story is done, finished, complete and wrapped up. But... <em>now</em> I understand the meaning of a "twisted HEA". Don't be scared off, it's still 100% a HEA, guys. I <em>promise</em>. But it's just..... a leeeeetle bit twisted. It's hard to explain without spoilers so I'm going to be very vague here but it was very "interesting" to get inside Jake's head -- he was this amazing guy, protective to an extreme, willing to go to <em>any</em> lengths to keep his family safe. <em>Any. Lengths. </em>He wasn't a danger to society or anything but the epilogue was borderline creepy... Um, lets just say that I am reeeeeeally glad he was a good guy 'cuz the world would be a scary as fuck place with him in it as a bad guy. But I can say that I absolutely fell for him. I loved him and I loved his role in Abby's life. I loved how protective he was and how <em>much</em> he loved her because that much was undeniable. That man <em>loved</em> Abby - body and soul.<br><br>This really was a fantastic read!! I love books that push the envelope and step outside the box. I love the unpredictability of not knowing where the book will turn next. This book took me on a crazy, emotional, gritty ride and I loved the whole thing. I couldn't put it down and didn't want to stop reading.<br><br>I'd highly recommend adding it to your reading lists :)<br><br><strong>Rating: 4.5 stars</strong> (4 stars for the first half of the book, but then there were definitely 5 star moments for me in the second, so overall I'm going with 4.5 stars)<br><br>CASTING (see above and below)<br><img width='100%"' src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384658396i/6926044._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width='100%"' src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384658396i/6926045.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br></b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" href="/user/show/52207144">♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ</a>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781620152690" href="/book/show/44137138-the-dark-light-of-day">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2078578529" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9705674656219670575"><u>5 Broken soul to broken soul. ★'s</u> <br/><br/><i>“We were just us, broken and bruised, fucked-up and messy, and together we were everything we never thought we could be.”</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Walking with a friend in the dark is better than walking alone in the light.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>My ♥Abby & Jake♥</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1535936606i/26243838._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>“I like the way you make the silence bearable.”</i><br/><br/><i>“I was in love with the angel and in lust with the devil. If I were honest with myself, I'd have to say that I was in love with the devil, too.”</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1535689631i/26227076._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><i>*Warning: contains disturbing situations, graphic viole</i></span>
  <span id="freeText9705674656219670575" style="display:none"><u>5 Broken soul to broken soul. ★'s</u> <br><br><i>“We were just us, broken and bruised, fucked-up and messy, and together we were everything we never thought we could be.”</i><br><br><b>
  <i>“Walking with a friend in the dark is better than walking alone in the light.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>My ♥Abby &amp; Jake♥</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1535936606i/26243838._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I like the way you make the silence bearable.”</i><br><br><i>“I was in love with the angel and in lust with the devil. If I were honest with myself, I'd have to say that I was in love with the devil, too.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1535689631i/26227076._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><i>*Warning: contains disturbing situations, graphic violence, sex, strong language, drug use, and all types of abuse.*</i><br><br><b>~Reread~</b><br>This was even better the second time around! <i>The Dark Light of Day</i> is one of those books that will draw you in and hold you captive until you've read every last word on every last page. I was hook from the first chapter. Personally, I could <b>NOT</b> put it down to save my life. This book right here is what made me fall in love with <i>T.M. Frazier</i>, to begin with. From her writing to her world building and to her broken characters. Everything. Is. Just. Perfect. Plus the plot was unpredictable. This is not your typical love story. It's dark, twisted, brutal as hell, devastating, intense, raw and heart-shattering, with deeply broken characters but it's also absolutely freaking beautiful. This for reals broke me and I cried so many times 😭😭. Abby and Jake’s story is not easy... they both come from broken families and traumatic childhoods and they both have inner demons they have to work through. Abby's past is darker than you'll want to imagine and the shit she goes through will make you sick, piss you off and make you want to murder someone. Let's just say... she doesn't have an easy go at life, at every corner something or someone is knocking her down but she always comes back swinging. Let me tell you, Abby is one Resilient chick and I fell in love with her character. I was so entranced by Abby and Jakes story even though it gutted me to my very core. I loved watching there love story unfold and seeing two broken people find themselves in each other. I completely fell in love with Jake 😍, *sigh* he's just so swoony and his dark side was very alluring. ♥Abby and Jake♥ are one of my most favorite couples. <i>The Dark Light of Day</i> is one of those books I could happily read over and over again and know with certainty that I'll love it even more than the last! If you're looking for something tragically beautiful then this is for you and I highly recommend if you haven't yet read this do so ASAP! You won't be disappointed and if you are... well then you're insane 😉! <br><b>This will keep you at-the-edge-of-your-seat!!</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1535689631i/26227076._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I fell asleep that night in the arms of a killer. I'd never slept better.”</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1536019848ra/26248436.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“For the first time in a long time a bit of something I was unfamiliar with crept up inside me.<br>If I hadn’t known better, I’d have thought it was hope.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1535689631i/26227076._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I finally realized that it’s possible to love within a space that sometimes holds nothing but emptiness.. or nothing but darkness.<br>After all, we all have darkness within us.<br>Some of us more than others.”</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1536019848ra/26248437.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Sick, twisted Abby was in love with the sick, twisted, beautiful Jake.”</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13353689165329951447"><b>5 Dark and Utterly Captivating Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384623046i/6918854._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>Walking with a friend in the dark is better than walking alone in the light.</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384623046ra/6918855.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384373253i/6859983.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Do you like sweet romances? Rainbows? Unicorns? Perfectly normal and non-damaged MC? Well too fucking bad! Because you're not going to get that here. Not even close. So prepare yourself for a story that's dark, gritty, brutal, devastating, gut-wrenching, keep-you-at-the-edge-of-your-seat-wanting-to-see-what-happens-next. Can't say you weren't warned.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384624668ra/6919160.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Want me to describe my feelings </span>
  <span id="freeText13353689165329951447" style="display:none"><b>5 Dark and Utterly Captivating Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384623046i/6918854._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>Walking with a friend in the dark is better than walking alone in the light.</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384623046ra/6918855.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384373253i/6859983.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Do you like sweet romances? Rainbows? Unicorns? Perfectly normal and non-damaged MC? Well too fucking bad! Because you're not going to get that here. Not even close. So prepare yourself for a story that's dark, gritty, brutal, devastating, gut-wrenching, keep-you-at-the-edge-of-your-seat-wanting-to-see-what-happens-next. Can't say you weren't warned.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384624668ra/6919160.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Want me to describe my feelings through this books in one gif? <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396987ra/765617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> If there was one phrase that was running through my mind the entire time I was reading it, it was 'Holy shit!' I couldn't believe this was a debut novel. Brilliantly written, utterly captivating, the story of Abby and Jake stole my heart, broke me, gutted me, and kept me completely unable to put the book down until I finished. I was sucked in from the very first chapter.<br><br>Abby...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384623718i/6918960.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>How a person can survive the horrors that this poor girl goes through and still come out with the strength that she does is beyond me. Life has not been kind to Abby. Not in the least. But with everything that she goes through, she maintains this persevering core. I fell in love with her character. You would think someone like her would be shy, awkward, but every time life knocked her down, she came up swinging. She didn't take shit from anyone, but the vulnerable, damaged, and scared little girl that she hides behind her her carefully constructed walls broke my heart.<br><br>Jake...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384624668i/6919161._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>He was just everything you love in a broken hero. Jake is a man that has some very dark demons. He's not the white knight that rides into the night to save Abby, but he does in his own dark way. But what I truly loved, was that mostly Abby saves herself.<br><br>This is not a story of perfect love and romance. It's a story about 2 damaged souls that learn to walk together in the shadows.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384373253i/6859983.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>By the time I finished this book, I was a fucked up mess of emotions. This book does not let up for even a second. I spent the entire second half of this book a hysterical fucking mess. And when I was down, and thinking it can't possibly get any worse, T.M. Frazier would take what I imagined is her 6in booted foot and kick me right in the damn feels.<br>It was<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384624668ra/6919162.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Followed by<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/612690.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Which mainly led to me feeling like<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384625429ra/6919436.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book gutted me. Gutted.Me. But I loved every single fucked up second of me. My advice for you once you decide to read this incredible yet dark story? Lots of booze. No really. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381349272ra/4740804.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You're going to need it.<br><br>This is an author that is now on my auto-buy list. I'm surprised I haven't seen this book more on my GR feeds. It deserves to be there. If you like dark and gritty romances, this book is a HUGE rec from this girl. And this is coming from one picky bitch.<br><br>Now if you'll excuse me, I'm off to set my feels right. They're completely FUBAR after I finished. And I thank you<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755439.gif" alt="" width="365" height="206" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i> ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <span id="freeText645372543640431743" style="display:none"><i>5 beautiful silence stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Walking with a friend in the dark is better than walking alone in the light.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434345046i/15207560.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Abby is tired of having to survive and just wants to <i>live</i>. Taking her life into her own hands, she decides to dodges the system just for a few more weeks until her 18th birthday. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434344832i/15207547._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However when she is run out of her home by the case worker, she ends up with a gun pointed at her head when she is caught sleeping in her deceased grandma's truck. Abby takes Jake by surprise, and in him she finds a kindred spirit. It isn't easy but Jake <s>wants</s> needs to take care of Abby, wanting to scare away the demons that haunt her within.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I like the way you make the silence bearable.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434344832ra/15207548.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Abby and Jake share a bond of silence and companionship, sure there is an underlying sense of want, need and lust, but it is the likeness of their battered soul that makes them take notice of how far under their skin they have gone. Abby has her demons to fight and what she quickly realizes is that Jake has his own too, only his may be darker. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Together, we were just us. Battered and broken. Dark and difficult. Impulsive and scared.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434344832i/15207549._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Can they help each other find the light within each other, when they can't see it within themselves? Can they trust in what they have or will it be the reason they run and hide... <br><br><b>The Dark Light of Day</b> was simply amazing, heartbreakingly difficult to read at times, making me mad at the injustice and hurt that Abby had to live through. You'd think that she paid the ultimate price during her childhood, you'd think that was enough, but No... not even close. Abby is a survivor, resilient, she is so damn strong she focuses on what is important and tries to move on. Jake is a man whose world just got turned upside down, Abby makes him question every choice he has ever made. My heart broke so many times, and I even jumped on the bandwagon of willing bodily harm on the story's evil-asshole.<br><br>I can not tell you how much this standalone book sucked me in, I've had it for a while waiting patiently for me on my kindle and I immediately apologized for making it wait. Totally recommended for those who can handle the dark, but can find the light within the story. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="645372543640431743" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6272462010010352" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Heart Attack Inducing</b>--Stars!!!<br><br>I think I had like 5 heart attacks while reading this book!         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728794320" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11986283085445486178"> Price drop to $.99 on Amazon for a short time!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382938581i/6291057.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yeesh, what a wild ride. Whew!!!<br/><br/>Abby...a seventeen year old girl literally scarred by life...her parents drug addicts who neglected, beat, and tortured her. <br/><b>
  <blockquote>"I didn't consider myself suicidal. Just tired."</blockquote>
</b> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382938581i/6291058.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>She hides from the world the scars on</span>
  <span id="freeText11986283085445486178" style="display:none"> Price drop to $.99 on Amazon for a short time!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382938581i/6291057.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeesh, what a wild ride. There were moments of pure New Adult drama, sugary sweet luv, and then BAM...I was blindsided by a completely different second half...sort of a Natural Born Killers feeling at times, and it totally rocked. Whew!!!<br><br>Abby...a seventeen year old girl literally scarred by life...her parents drug addicts who neglected, beat, and tortured her. <br><b>
  <blockquote>"I didn't consider myself suicidal. Just tired."</blockquote>
</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382938581i/6291058.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She hides from the world the scars on her body and can't stand physical contact, even by the one person who loves her, her Nan. Until one day, her Nan is suddenly gone, dead in a freak accident that leaves Abby alone in the world. Again.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"During my entire life, nobody had wanted me on my very best day on my very best behavior. <br>Nan wanted me at my worst, and sometimes, that was exactly what she got."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Then Abby meets Jake, the loner, mystery guy who's not much older than she is but with even less innocence in his eyes than she has.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382938581i/6291059.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's a bad boy meets lonely girl story, and I have to admit to being a bit hesitant about starting it. There are a couple of scenes that are very hard to swallow. If you are sensitive to rape, steer clear or skim that part, because it's pretty bad. However, it's all relevant and necessary to the story; in fact, it sets the entire plotline up so it's not just thrown in for drama's sake. <br><br><u>WHAT I LOVED:</u><br>I loved how Abby and Jake were kindred souls more than just spiritually. There is a bit of insta love going on here, but I think maybe it was due to their situation and their mutual respect for one another than anything else. And that was a somewhat different take on it. Jake and Abby sort of meet up by chance, but their chance meeting leads to so much more. <i>I love that their story is never one of overwhelming hearts and flowers. This is a couple really just not meant to have that kind of love story. Theirs is tough and resilient, but never easy.</i><br><b>
  <blockquote>"What would happen when he got bored and tired of my sickeness, of my sadness and sorrow?"</blockquote>
</b><br>When Jake sort of overrides Abby's instict to hold back simply by paying attention to her, and showing her love before ever acting on it: case in point, the camera <b>and the time he spends</b> with her. This was the only real magic in their story, and it is what kept me holding on to Jake when the crazy starts to happen.<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382972666i/6310234.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <blockquote>"What's going on with us? It's important. I need to know now because at some point I'm not going to be able to give you what you want. And then what?"<br>He nuzzled his nose into my neck. "What is it you think I want?"<br>"Normal boy-girl stuff," I said throwing my hands in the air. I felt defeated before this line of conversation had even gotten started.<br>"That's where you're wrong. I don't want normal. I want you..."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Abby and Jake really need this passion and this devotion later when the crazy really goes down.<br><b>:(:(:(:(:(:(</b><br><u>WHAT I DIDN'T LOVE:</u><br>Gotta be honest- the first half of this book was just okay for me. It read very much like every other NA book out there, with a lot of drama, love too quickly, and all the trappings of young people feeling too much with their bodies and not enough with their heads. I was getting a little worried for a minute, but I shouldn't have because after the halfway mark, the REAL story kicks in and I remained glued to the pages. Another thing that I felt was lacking was more character development for Jake. He was a pretty volatile guy, and overreacted quite a bit. His actions were often more OTT than Abby's, which is quite the switch. <br><b>:(:(:(:(:(:(</b> <br><br>Back to what I loved: Without spoiling, I just want to point out the situation that Abby finds herself in and the resulting life that she leads was WONDERFULLY done, and added so much gravity to this book. It's truly what made it for me. The town that has treated her so horribly, the family of cops/judges/lawyers that took her options away from her, and her revenge for the atrocities were the really gripping part of this book. And the little twisted pleasure that both Abby and Jake got out of exacting their revenge gave me my own little sick sense of twisted pleasure: yet another author who can make me feel things I usually try to avoid, lol. But it was awesome.<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382973680i/6310922._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>One thing that I though was interesting was how the book begins with a chapter from Jake's point of view and also ends with a chapter from his point of view, sandwiching the meat of the story, which was Abby's POV. Really cool way to do it without switching constantly. I LOVED IT!!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/quotes/1377797852p8/506461.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Final review now posted<br>Copy provided by the author and her representative.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11986283085445486178" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13789319855969546591"><b>I LOVE ABBY & JAKE!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382039884i/5605275._SX540_.jpg' width='405' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book had a profound impact on me. Simply put, it made me feel. I had <b>KNOTS</b> in my stomach throughout the whole story. There is no way I can’t give this one 5 Stars. I can’t say that the story was perfection, or that the characters were, but I <b>LOVED</b> it!! <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“We were just us, broken and bruised, fucked-up and messy, and together we were everything we never thought we could be.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>This is one of those stories where you just want to talk about it. Perhaps it’s the shock factor?</span>
  <span id="freeText13789319855969546591" style="display:none"><b>I LOVE ABBY &amp; JAKE!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382039884i/5605275._SX540_.jpg" width="405" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book had a profound impact on me. Simply put, it made me feel. I had <b>KNOTS</b> in my stomach throughout the whole story. There is no way I can’t give this one 5 Stars. I can’t say that the story was perfection, or that the characters were, but I <b>LOVED</b> it!! <br><br><b>
  <i>“We were just us, broken and bruised, fucked-up and messy, and together we were everything we never thought we could be.” </i>
</b><br><br>This is one of those stories where you just want to talk about it. Perhaps it’s the shock factor? Or Jake? Or Abby? Or Frank? <br><br>The story was <b>DISTURBING, GRAPHIC, BROKEN, HEARTBREAKING, and truly ADDICTIVE.</b> Honestly, I never knew what lengths the author would go to, she definitely kept me on my toes. Even when I predicted some of the twists, the impact was nonetheless devastating. <br><br>Abby and Jake had me from the start. This isn’t your typical love story and it was on the <b>TWISTED</b> side, but the romance was captivating. <br><br><b>
  <i>“That’s where you’re wrong. I don’t want normal. I want you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Kudos to T.M. Frazier for her debut novel and I’ll be looking any future stories she releases.<br><br>I would gladly read more about these two...in case T.M. Frazier has any thoughts on a follow up book.<br><br>That epilogue...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380740097ra/3117713.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*Copy kindly provided by <b>T.M. Frazier</b> in exchange for an honest review* </span>

    <a title="Sabrina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina"><img alt="Sabrina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1392065462p2/18085807.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/723446634?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/18085807-sabrina">Sabrina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/31178025-the-dark-light-of-day">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=deliciously-tattooed-pierced">deliciously-tattooed-pierced</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18085807-sabrina?shelf=give-it-to-me-dark-and-twisted">give-it-to-me-dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer723446634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9964355698347963138">Get it FREE! <br/><a href='https://amzn.to/2swhoRM%22' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> * <a href='https://amzn.to/2U4q5yu' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Re read: June 18, 2015<br/>2nd re read: January 18, 2019</i>
</b><br/><br/><b> Sick, twisted Abby was in love with the sick, twisted, beautiful Jake. </b><br/><br/>This is not your normal love story, no, this is a story of how dark true love can be. A story of two tortured souls coming together and fighting to survive after their tragic pasts. Neither Jake or Abby are perfect, but they are perfect together. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425113i/848064.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Abby was a broken, down on her luck, sleeping in a junkyard, 17 year old girl when she met J</span>
  <span id="freeText9964355698347963138" style="display:none">Get it FREE! <br><a href="https://amzn.to/2swhoRM%22" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> * <a href="https://amzn.to/2U4q5yu" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a><br><br><b>
  <i>Re read: June 18, 2015<br>2nd re read: January 18, 2019</i>
</b><br><br><b> Sick, twisted Abby was in love with the sick, twisted, beautiful Jake. </b><br><br>This is not your normal love story, no, this is a story of how dark true love can be. A story of two tortured souls coming together and fighting to survive after their tragic pasts. Neither Jake or Abby are perfect, but they are perfect together. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425113i/848064.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Abby was a broken, down on her luck, sleeping in a junkyard, 17 year old girl when she met Jake. Barely surviving her painful past, and now losing her Nan, the first person to actually care for her, she starts to give up on life. Enter Jake, who gives her something to live for, something to survive for. <br><br>Jake needs Abby just as much as she needs him, though. Because Jake has secrets, secrets that make him believe he isn't worthy of Abby's love. Even though he thinks he doesn't deserve Abby, he will do anything to have her, even kill for her. Together they make a love so damaged, and so imperfect that there is no denying this is the story of true love. <br><br><b> We were just us. Broken and bruised. Fucked up and messy. And together we were everything we never thought we could be. </b><br><br>I loved this story. It was so dark and twisted and yet somehow really beautiful at the same time. I was rooting Jake and Abby the whole time and just wanted to see them get their HEA. The story of how they got there was so intriguing and I could not put this down. I dropped everything to read and finish this book, and I regret not one second.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9964355698347963138" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=2013-faves">2013-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=biker">biker</a>
          </div>
