        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer712084776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18017749778292963644"><b>“After all, we all have darkness within us”</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380736834ra/3117097.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>FIVE BIG- this is what I crave in a book Stars Plus…</b><br/><br/>I loved this one. It has some of the best elements of what I want in a great read. Deep, disturbing and dark characters, kickass hero and heroine, witty and snarky humor, suspense, healing love and a keep-me-on-the-edge-till-the-end storyline! <br/><br/>This is a debut novel, people and <b>Wow…</b> I am so looking forward to more from this author.<br/><br/>From the gut wrenching opening scene in Jake’s POV to the epilogue, <b>
  <u>Th</u></b></span>
  <span id="freeText18017749778292963644" style="display:none"><b>“After all, we all have darkness within us”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380736834ra/3117097.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FIVE BIG- this is what I crave in a book Stars Plus…</b><br><br>I loved this one. It has some of the best elements of what I want in a great read. Deep, disturbing and dark characters, kickass hero and heroine, witty and snarky humor, suspense, healing love and a keep-me-on-the-edge-till-the-end storyline! <br><br>This is a debut novel, people and <b>Wow…</b> I am so looking forward to more from this author.<br><br>From the gut wrenching opening scene in Jake’s POV to the epilogue, <b>
  <u>This. Book. Owned. Me.</u>
</b> <br><br>The description and detail in which the author wrote about the town of Coral Pines, Florida and all of Jake and Abby’s life experiences had me feeling, smelling, seeing every scene in stomach fluttering and heart skipping imagery. <br><br>I can't begin to scratch the surface of what this story is about because there is so much and I do not want to give anything away. I read this one with just a vague idea of what to expect and I am so happy I got the full experience. This may not be for everyone, but if you are looking for a raw, gritty, harsh yet amazingly written and uniquely beautiful love story- then I would highly recommend this one. <br><br>Jake and Bee and many of the secondary characters will be characters I remember for a very long time and I will be reading this book again.<br><br><b>Some favorite quotes:</b><br><br>*<b>“I was pretty sure that the man with the beautiful blue eyes, the temper and the big sexy bike—the very man who I had heard getting sucked off in a junkyard little more than twenty-four hours ago, mere moments before he put a gun to my head—had just adopted me"</b><br><br>*<b>“Rent is payable in ass and grass only, baby”</b><br><br>*<b>“That’s where you’re wrong. I don’t want normal. I want you”</b><br><br>*<b>“I wanted to take on his pain because he’d taken mine so completely”</b><br><br>*<b>“How could broken plus broken ever equal whole?”</b><br><br>*<b>“Make him suffer, baby,” I whispered to no one”</b><br><br>This book takes a spot on my favorites shelf of 2013! <b>FANTASTIC!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380736834ra/3117098.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>TO Read Next?...</b><br> <br></span>

<div id="review_743171664" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/743171664" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/743171664?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20256653-the-dark-light-of-day">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-dark-contemporary">new-adult-dark-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=suspence">suspence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=august-2015">august-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=series-book">series-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=romantic-suspence">romantic-suspence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer743171664" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17397326975899774647">"Walking with a friend in the dark is better than walking alone in the light."<br/><br/>I don't even know where to begin with this one. I adored this story, and yet there were times it was so hard and gruesome to read I didn't know if I had the courage to continue. It reminds me of another book I read recently where the bad is really horrific, but when the good happens...it is beyond beautiful! This was that kind of book for me, and I absolutely fell in love with Jake and Abby; even their twisted broken s</span>
  <span id="freeText17397326975899774647" style="display:none">"Walking with a friend in the dark is better than walking alone in the light."<br /><br />I don't even know where to begin with this one. I adored this story, and yet there were times it was so hard and gruesome to read I didn't know if I had the courage to continue. It reminds me of another book I read recently where the bad is really horrific, but when the good happens...it is beyond beautiful! This was that kind of book for me, and I absolutely fell in love with Jake and Abby; even their twisted broken souls..every inch of them I savoured. Yes, they were not two healthy individuals; but in my eyes they were both warriors who had walked through the flames and had the scars to show it. Even with their trauma, that they could find one another and be able to love so deeply was nothing short of amazing to me. That they accepted each other for who they were--not just the good parts; but the parts that were down right evil at times, it just made their love that much more powerful to me. <br /><br />A lot of author's have a hard time pulling off a character like Jake. One that has such a tormented soul, and is evil because of it; but allows his heart to be consumed by the love he feels for his woman. When Jake first encountered Abby, it was love at first sight for him, and it was that all consuming and possessive love that for some reason I just soak it all up. T.M Frazier does such a great job of writing an anti-hero that is impossible not to love. I enjoy her writing style as well, and I know when I read one of her books I am in for a roller coaster ride of feels. With this book, I can honestly say that I felt I had a front row seat to some of the experiences of the characters. This was not easy to be a witness to. At one point, I had to stop because I felt physically ill by what Abby had just gone through. I wasn't sure if I could get over it, however; I pulled up my big girl panties and kept reading and I'm so glad that I did. Once you hit rock bottom, there is no way but up from there! Once the upward slope came, I was satisfied with how the story went and the good feels that came along with it.<br /><br />I read this story because of meeting Jake and Abby briefly in the author's other book; Tyrant. I was immediately intrigued by this man who to those who don't know him well is a monster. The few that are close to him though, know underneath the monster their is a man who love very deeply. I needed to find out more about this couple. When I realized that their book had already been written, I just had to check it out! What an experience it was. I won't ever forget this couple who were so broken, and yet when they came together they made themselves whole! This is a must read! It isn't an easy read at times; but it is so worth the heartache...believe me..I will cherish this story always, it was just so special.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17397326975899774647" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer744936557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2476502796556216360"><i>
  <b>Did I love this book? Yes... Did it completely fuck with my head and cause me to lose my shit several times.. hell to the fucking yes!! Holyshit!!</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381039646ra/3936828.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>My emotions!!! OHMYGOD... it was like the rpm's on my heart were way past the safe level for the majority of this story. <br/><br/><br/> This book popped up on my feeds late this afternoon and I knew, immediately, that I had to read it.... I JUST HAD TO READ IT. So here I am.. 2:00 in the morning and I've just finished it. Literaly.. could not put this book down.</span>
  <span id="freeText2476502796556216360" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>Did I love this book? Yes... Did it completely fuck with my head and cause me to lose my shit several times.. hell to the fucking yes!! Holyshit!!</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381039646ra/3936828.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>My emotions!!! OHMYGOD... it was like the rpm's on my heart were way past the safe level for the majority of this story. <br><br><br> This book popped up on my feeds late this afternoon and I knew, immediately, that I had to read it.... I JUST HAD TO READ IT. So here I am.. 2:00 in the morning and I've just finished it. Literaly.. could not put this book down. From page one , PAGE ONE, this book pretty much owned me and didn't let me go until the very end. This was gritty, intense, disgusting, fucked up, and crazy. <br><br>Abby.. jeez this poor girl went through so much hell in her short life. By 17 she's seen shit and been through shit that is just way wayyyy past crazy. How this girl didn't cave in and land in a loony bin someplace is just beyond me. But all the hell that life thew at her just made her stronger. She roll's with the punches.. and damn.. those punches keep coming and coming and coming.....then one day she finally hits that brick wall and it's all about to cave in on her..... <br><br><i>
  <b>Abby....</b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382253866i/5773013.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jake.. sexy and a little twisted.. He's not a good guy... he's bad, does bad things and doesn't give a shit about anyone. He's got some serious scar damage on his soul that sucked him down years ago and it turned him into the man he is today.. a man with secrets. Deadly secrets... <br><br><br><i>
  <b> Jake....</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382254582i/5773288._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jake finds Abby when she's at her lowest point and something about her just makes him want to help her through whatever it is she's going through. It doesn't take long for him to realize the wants to slay all her dragons. He'd do anything for her... It's a feeling he's never had before and he's not really very good at it. He's not very trusting and well.. dude totally pissed me the hell off worse than any book guy before I think.. seriously..<br><br> I was total raging.. I had to put my Kindle down and step away for a good 20 minutes at one point. You see, I love my Kindle and I was real close to throwing it across the room. Once I started cursing at it, I knew it was time for me to take a moment and step back. I think the fact that the shit totally hit the fan in such a way so quickly, that I just am still wigging out about it a bit. <br><br>You know, that moment in a book where you start getting a bit nervous, things are going good but you start hearing the jaws music in the back ground.. your brain is sending out warning signals...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382255435ra/5773670.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Well... my brain was sending the signals so I was turning the pages slowly.. and then BAM!!<br><br><i>
  <b>What the fucking fuck.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382255435ra/5773671.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And if it wasn't enough to totally DESTROY me.. lets poor a nice dose WHY WHY WHY WHY WHY WHY WHY THE FUCK WHY WHY WHY on top...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382255725ra/5773811.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And then.. just when my brain is total goo and I'm just shaking my head and freaking the fuck out I get one more big thump to my head. <br><br>By this time... it was time for ...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382255725ra/5773812.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382255725ra/5773813.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is my recommendation that you have alcohol handy while reading this on. Seriously. Completely sober is not the way to go. At least for me it wasn't. Damn. <br><br>OK.. So even though my mind got fucked and my heart got bruised.... it was totally worth it. Completely worth it. There was a good stretch of hell to go through.. but the ending was wrapped up in a really good way . And although I can't say I had a smile on my face at the end, I did have a very satisfied feeling. Abby and Jake go through hell and back.. but the journey was insanely good. <br><br>I had to give this book 5 stars because any book that can pull that many emotions out of me totally deserves it. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2729854237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15322962983346881122"><strong>I expected Jake to be a bit darker!</strong><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1586567311i/29270930._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I read this after reading the first seven books of the King series. I was really interested in hearing Jake’s story after reading so much about him in those books. He is such an emotionless killing machine in those books. He gets off on the blood, killing and even torture.<br/><br/>So I was a bit surprised at how nice he was to Abby when he first meets her and how normal he is. Also how quickly he falls in love with her. I expected him to be a little more like Dexter. No</span>
  <span id="freeText15322962983346881122" style="display:none"><strong>I expected Jake to be a bit darker!</strong><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1586567311i/29270930._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I read this after reading the first seven books of the King series. I was really interested in hearing Jake’s story after reading so much about him in those books. He is such an emotionless killing machine in those books. He gets off on the blood, killing and even torture.<br><br>So I was a bit surprised at how nice he was to Abby when he first meets her and how normal he is. Also how quickly he falls in love with her. I expected him to be a little more like Dexter. Not that he isn’t dark, he is certainly that. He also eventually admits that he is a hired killer. <br><br>The story was very good though. Abby’s background and what she goes through is very much the focus in this even more than Jake. He is a good man for Abby. Overall I really liked the story. I guess I was just hoping for a bit more dark and twisty. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1586478437ra/29263641.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.ilikebooksbest.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a>|<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/wennel" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a>|<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>|<a href="https://www.instagram.com/ilikebooksbest" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a>|<a href="https://www.twitter.com/wendysu020202" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>|<a href="https://www.bookbub.com/profile/1895823057" rel="nofollow noopener">BookBub</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1699788488?book_show_action=true">Jul 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=crime-mafia">crime-mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=2contemporary-lovestories">2contemporary-lovestories</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1699788488" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5056919995437749125">TM Frazier does not hesitate to torture her female characters until they reach their breaking point and then she lets them been tortured a bit more until they reach a new limit. And only then she lets them rise from their ashes like a phoenix and live as normal and happy as they should live.<br/>I started this book because I got a glimpse of Jake at King's books and he looked interesting in a twisted short of way. I wanted to learn more about him. I cannot say I understood his actions, his behaviour </span>
  <span id="freeText5056919995437749125" style="display:none">TM Frazier does not hesitate to torture her female characters until they reach their breaking point and then she lets them been tortured a bit more until they reach a new limit. And only then she lets them rise from their ashes like a phoenix and live as normal and happy as they should live.<br />I started this book because I got a glimpse of Jake at King's books and he looked interesting in a twisted short of way. I wanted to learn more about him. I cannot say I understood his actions, his behaviour with this book. Instead, I learnt a lot about Abby, the girl he fell in love with. She was strong, self contained, life inspiring. I am glad I read her story and I am glad she let Jake in her life. It was the best thing it could happen to him.<br />The book was hard to read -even painful sometimes- but it is definitely life inspiring and is worth every second you will spend reading it.</span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer711448449" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7510997434195097227"><b>4 Surviving, Darkly Shining Stars<br/><br/><i>We may not have been perfect, or even acceptable by anyone else’s standards. But together, we were perfect. Together, we were just us. Battered and broken. Dark and difficult. Impulsive and scared. Everything we never thought we could be.<i></i></i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388170451i/7755012.jpg' width='400' height='160' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In our souls, darkness and light co-exist. Sometimes one of them prevails, but the darkness never totally consumes the light. A precarious balance holds the threads of our sanity and mends the broken pieces of our battered bodies</span>
  <span id="freeText7510997434195097227" style="display:none"><b>4 Surviving, Darkly Shining Stars<br><br><i>We may not have been perfect, or even acceptable by anyone else’s standards. But together, we were perfect. Together, we were just us. Battered and broken. Dark and difficult. Impulsive and scared. Everything we never thought we could be.<i></i></i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388170451i/7755012.jpg" width="400" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In our souls, darkness and light co-exist. Sometimes one of them prevails, but the darkness never totally consumes the light. A precarious balance holds the threads of our sanity and mends the broken pieces of our battered bodies. Life in all its glory is cruel but people aren't meant to be alone. Only lonely for a while.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407444ra/795800.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is our story. A tale of abuse and unimaginable pain. Of love and chances. Of killers and teenagers. Of falling 7 times and getting up 8. A story about death and the love that defines us.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406082i/791813.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Abby</b> could be a normal 17-year old. But not all teenagers had junkies parents who abused their child for their next fix. Not all kids spent a childhood of horror and they forever bear the scars inside and out to prove that they survived it.<br><br><i>
  <b>I didn’t consider myself suicidal. Just tired.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406082i/791814.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Tired of defending herself against the prejudice she daily lives, a death of the only person she ever claimed her own, will drive her to new path. To the love of a lifetime and one last horror that she will have to overcome with her head high. Another damaged soul, will be her only chance a happiness. Dare she claim it or life once again will betray her?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417579i/826112.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Jake</b> is a killer. Forced to leave his home when his father blamed him for his brother death he lets the pain and hate consume him and he becomes a hired gun. A ruthless man that deals in death. This man will see in Abby what everyone else failed to see so far. Her beauty inside. Together they dreamt, but human nature drew them apart. Does he deserve a second chance and will he become the vengeance she so much needs?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401123ra/778004.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Dark, emotional, haunting and disturbing this story is not for the faint of heart. This a brutal tale of love and hate that will break your heart and force you to accept that life is unforgiving and happiness comes in all shapes and sizes. Abby and Jake are broken beyond repair but you root for them and cry and despair. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5769238.T_M__Frazier" title="T.M. Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">T.M. Frazier</a> pulls no punches. She delivers a solid read that will stay with you forever. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388170451ra/7755013.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716458730" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer89518234404179847"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601662i/8249840._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601662i/8249841._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What the fuck?! Lol! This book is bat shit crazy! And I'm feeling a little warped, because I really enjoyed it! I do love a book that makes me double-check that my moral compass is still pointing in the right direction!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I fell asleep that night in the arms of a killer. I'd never slept better.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>4.5 stars for Bee & Jake!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601774i/8249895.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So, I love a good biker romance. It's such a guilty pleasure, reading about the depravity, corruption and extortion. The criminal activity, the killings... The things most</span>
  <span id="freeText89518234404179847" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601662i/8249840._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601662i/8249841._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What the fuck?! Lol! This book is bat shit crazy! And I'm feeling a little warped, because I really enjoyed it! I do love a book that makes me double-check that my moral compass is still pointing in the right direction!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I fell asleep that night in the arms of a killer. I'd never slept better.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>4.5 stars for Bee &amp; Jake!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601774i/8249895.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I love a good biker romance. It's such a guilty pleasure, reading about the depravity, corruption and extortion. The criminal activity, the killings... The things most of us (with any luck) will never come across in real life but lap up, with a twisted kind of fascination, from the books we read.<br><br>And <i>The Dark Light of Day</i> certainly didn't disappoint. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Sick, twisted Abby was in love with the sick, twisted, beautiful Jake.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Abby is the child of two abusive, junkie, waste-of-space parents. With her mother behind bars, when her father is found dead, Abby is sent to live with her Nan. But tragedy strikes again when Abby's Nan dies in a freak accident and she is left homeless and alone. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601662i/8249842._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When she meets Jake, the dangerous, tattooed, sexy-as-hell badass biker who won't be tied down by roots, and has a past and secrets as dark as hers, Abby's life changes forever. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Even though life hands you a big pile of shit, you don't have to roll around in it and make shit angels.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Abby is a total bitch. She's sarcastic, un-trusting, cynical, defensive, has walls as impenetrable as Alcatraz and you can't help but love her. Can you blame her? The girl's been abused, neglected, abandoned and left with terrible scars, inside and out. And she's only 17! But I really rather liked her. I liked her snarky attitude and her sharp tongue. I liked that she didn't take any shit. We read so many female characters that won't say boo to a goose, so I always enjoy when we meet a heroine with balls as big as her heroes. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601663i/8249843.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Fuck anyone who thinks anything on someone like you could ever be anything beautiful. You should be proud of them, baby."<br>"Proud?"<br>"Yes, proud. They make you powerful. Each line is a road travelled, an experience you had, whether it was good or bad. Each mark is proof of pain in the past, not the present. You are a survivor, you are a warrior. These are the scalps hanging from your fucking belt. You took the beatings and here you are, in front of me. You are fucking amazing."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Let me tell you about Jake... He's a killer. There's no beating around the bush, no grey areas... straight up, Jake kills people. And he isn't ashamed or embarrassed about it either. And I loved him, too! He has a past he'd rather forget, a regularly 'itchy trigger finger' and has experienced his own fair share of loss and heartache, that has led him down the path he has taken. But he has a good heart. The way he cares for Abby shows us, early on, that Jake is a good man, deep down. I love how he calls her 'Bee' and the gentle banter between them. I loved how he was both forceful and gentle with her, in equal measures, coaxing her to face her fears and reveal her secrets.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Why do I want to touch you? Are you fucking kidding me right now? I want to help you. I want to hold you. I want to make it all okay for you. I want to fucking touch you because you are the most beautiful person I've ever seen, and I can't imagine never being able to hold your hand or kiss you. And yes - I want to fuck you, too, like I've never wanted anything in my whole life."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601663i/8249844.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One thing that bothered me about this book was the speed that Abby and Jake got together. With hindsight, I can see that the author wrote the book this way because there was so much of Jake and Abby's story to tell after the initial getting together. But still, whilst I was reading it I was thinking 'woah, ok, that was quick'! And whilst so much of this book was so raw and so real, this little issue kind of diluted that realness for me. However, it's a minor point and on the whole, I really enjoyed the story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We may not have been perfect, or even acceptable by anyone else's standards. But together, we were perfect.<br>Together, we were just us.<br>Battered and broken. Dark and difficult. Impulsive and scared.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Whilst the first half of this book intrigued me, from about 50% onwards, I really could not put this down. It was on a roll. T.M. Frazier pulls no punches with <i>The Dark Light of Day</i>. She isn't afraid of writing scenes that will cause controversy or offend some readers. The story is gritty and graphic. I really felt Abby's pain and there is one scene, where T.M. Frazier is describing bodily injuries, where the writing gave me such clear mental visuals, which was both shocking and evocative. So if you are at all squeamish, easily offended or aren't quick to forgive minor misgivings like blows people's brains out on a regular basis, probably best you don't touch this book with a very long barge pole. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601663i/8249845.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I would kill for you, Bee. Happily." He ran his fingers down my cheek. "I need you to know that."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><i>The Dark Light of Day</i> is full of plot twists that will have you on the edge of your seat. It's action packed, deep, dark and totally fucked up. It's a great example of our acceptance, as readers, of things in books that we would never even contemplate accepting in 'real life'. I read lots of books about controlling, alpha males and then the respective reviews moaning about how women shouldn't accept violence or control from men in books, etc. etc. However, this book, and others like it, just prove that reading books allows us to push our boundaries and flirt with situations we would balk at in reality. Situations, qualities and people that would disgust us, irritate us and even terrify us. I love that about reading and I really enjoyed that with <i>The Dark Light of Day</i>. Would I shack up with killer in real life? Of course I freakin' wouldn't! Did I love reading about Abby and her love for Jake? Yes! Did I find Jake sexy and dangerously desirable? Hell yes!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>A revenge kill is the best kind of kill.<br>But a revenge kill for your family, with your woman's permission?<br>That's borderline erotic. </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601663i/8249846._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is written from Abby's POV, with the exception of the prologue and epilogue and let me tell you, the epilogue, from Jake's POV, is so unbelievable twisted, it actually made me laugh a little. I was rolling my eyes like 'Jake, you crazy screwed-up, murdering motherfucker', lol! The ending of this book was perfectly in keeping with the rest of the story. It does have a happy ending. A fucked-up happy ending, but you come to expect that with Abby and Jake, and it's a happy ending, nonetheless. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601663i/8249847.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We were just us. Broken and bruised. Fucked up and messy. And together we were everything we never though we could be.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'd definitely recommend this book!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601663i/8249848._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>'The Dark Light of Day'</i> Statistics</b><br><b>• Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥<br><b>• Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>• Length:</b> 258 pages<br><b>• Narrative:</b> Mostly Abby's POV. Prologue &amp; epilogue from Jake's POV. Past tense.<br><b>• Series:</b> ✗ <br><b>• Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>• Themes:</b><br>Abuse<br>Crime<br><b>• WARNING. This book includes...</b> <br>Sexual content. Death. Rape. Abuse. Drug abuse. Violence.<br>Virtually everything you can think of that might need a warning label!<br><b>• Writing:</b> Good<br><br>Check out this review on my blog ➜ <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389786435i/8054383._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/The-Dark-Light-T-M-Frazier-ebook/dp/B00F8KMR8A/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1390601437&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=dark+light+of+day" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756313._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/The-Dark-Light-T-M-Frazier-ebook/dp/B00F8KMR8A/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1390601437&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=dark+light+of+day" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756314._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Like this review and want to keep up to date with more book news…?</b><br><blockquote>Follow me at the links below…</blockquote><br>My blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBook...</a></span>

<div id="review_2084843573" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2084843573" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2084843573?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/31178025-the-dark-light-of-day">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=3-star">3-star</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=neighbors-live-with">neighbors-live-with</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=separation-without-other-partners">separation-without-other-partners</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2084843573" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1688725637948733321"><b> 3 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I think I did it again 🤦🏻‍♀️ I had my expectations up way too high for this! I remember being so intruiged by this couple in the King series, and that along with all the raving reviews -- I was convinced that this would be a winner for me. Don't get me wrong -- I didn't hate it or anything, but I also didn't love it. I thought it was just ok. I teared up a few times, but I was expecting this mega angstfest that had me feeling the feels like crazy...and that just didn't h</span>
  <span id="freeText1688725637948733321" style="display:none"><b> 3 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I think I did it again 🤦🏻‍♀️ I had my expectations up way too high for this! I remember being so intruiged by this couple in the King series, and that along with all the raving reviews -- I was convinced that this would be a winner for me. Don't get me wrong -- I didn't hate it or anything, but I also didn't love it. I thought it was just ok. I teared up a few times, but I was expecting this mega angstfest that had me feeling the feels like crazy...and that just didn't happen. I also didn't like the instalove feeling I got. I wanted more development of feelings going on, because I honestly didn't feel the connection enough to believe the jump into "love". I also would've liked to experience some more happy times with them! I would still call it a HEA, but I am frustrated that we went through so much trauma and dark times with the two and got just a few happy times and a meh ending for it! There is a novella, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25224236.Dark_Needs__The_Dark_Light_of_Day___1_5_" title="Dark Needs (The Dark Light of Day, #1.5) by T.M. Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Needs</a>, out that might give us a little more of that, but I'm not all that eager to jump into it tbh 🤷🏻‍♀️<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Abby and Jake's story. Abby has had a horrible string of bad luck when her grandma dies, she finds out that she might have to enter foster care again, and that their house is in the process of being foreclosed. She meets Jake when she is sleeping in her grandma's truck at his dad's junkyard. They are both intruiged by each other, but have a lot of other things going on. After bumping into one another a few more times, Abby ends up moving in with Jake. Jake takes his time with Abby since they both have messed up pasts, and they fall in love. There are some past demons that are revealed, some traumatic events, a separation, and a few sexy times...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told mainly in Abby's POV with the prologue and epilogue in Jake's. I think it would've contributed a lot to have his pov more often, so we could understand his thoughts and motives better.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. The ending felt a little abrupt, but I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well otherwise.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of. I felt like the feelings came out of nowhere tbh. The H claims that it was love at first sight later on in the story.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Jake. I liked him. I liked how he was protective and patient he was with the h.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Abby. I liked her. I appreciated her strength and how she fought for herself.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate. I teared up a bit, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H pushes away at one point, but I would also say that he is the main pursuer of the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not that many scenes and not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Mentions of condoms being used, but I don't remember any mention of std statuses or previous practices for the H (the h was a virgin). There is mention that the OM did not use any protection when he raped the h. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There is an OM that is interested in the h and causes a good bit of drama for the couple. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> Kind of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is a scene at the beginning where the h overhears the H getting a bj from OW.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No <br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for ~4 years, but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Child abuse and molestation (off page - but through graphic mentions/memories), homelessness (on page), loss of a parental figure/sibling (on and off page), alcoholic parent (on page), drug addicted parent (off page - through mentions), suicide of parent (off page - through graphic mentions), rape/assault (on page), unexpected pregnancy (on page), violence/murder (off page - through graphic mention), the h was a virgin, and ~5 year age difference between the H and h. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had ok closure and what I would reluctantly call a HEA ending. There is a novella out that might give us a little more closure, but I'm not sure. I would've liked more time with them in this book experiencing their HEA, but we get a short epilogue instead <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are married <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> It was part of my kindle unlimited subscription.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one is probably <u>Not Safe</u> for most safety gang readers.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with the H and OW<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="1688725637948733321" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_733901492" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/733901492" />
    <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty"><img alt="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481371426p2/13273769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435712i/880437._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 They couldn't fucking break me Stars!</b><br/><br/>I have been struggling to find the right words. I want to do this book justice, but my inadequacy is weighing me down and has my mind blank. The Dark Light of Day is a perfect example of a story you need to experience with the characters. You need to just jump in and open you heart and soul to Abby's story. Life has not been easy on Abby, barely surviving her horrific childhood she finally finds a bit of love and happiness when she is placed in her gr</span>
  <span id="freeText11256192867704514438" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/8gm2GtR" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435712i/880437._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4.5 They couldn't fucking break me Stars!</b><br><br>I have been struggling to find the right words. I want to do this book justice, but my inadequacy is weighing me down and has my mind blank. The Dark Light of Day is a perfect example of a story you need to experience with the characters. You need to just jump in and open you heart and soul to Abby's story. Life has not been easy on Abby, barely surviving her horrific childhood she finally finds a bit of love and happiness when she is placed in her grandmother’s care. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You can do anything, baby girl. I promise, I will never lie to you. You are bright and beautiful and resilient. You can do anything.” –Nan. </i>
</b> <br><br>Although things are looking up, she still struggles with the darkness of her past. She alienates herself from most people, hiding the scars on the inside as well as the outside. Then tragedy strikes and once again Abby is left with nothing. Finding shelter in a junkyard she meets Jake, a blonde haired, blue-eyed biker, who decides to help her. Jake is also carrying around some dark secrets of his own. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Each mark is proof of pain in the past, not the present. You are a survivor, you are a warrior.”</i>
</b><br><br>Not only do Abby and Jake struggle with their past and trying to open up to one another. They also have outside forces trying to destroy the foundation they are building. Have they finally found someone to share the darkness with or will heartbreak destroy them once and for all?<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/4owPB3B" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435712i/880438.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I absolutely loved Abby, she is the embodiment of strength, courage, and resilience. And I LOVED it when she got pissed off! This is not an easy story to read. It is painful, yet beautiful. The first half of this story caught my attention; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ although I was apprehensive about the insta-love  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but I fell head over heels in love with the second half. I loved that Abby had a relationship with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Frank, and her eulogy for him broke my heart. “His biggest regret was not the loss of the dead, but the loss of the living,” <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I was completely captivated. That is all I can say I don’t want to spoil anything! This is a must read!<br><br><b>
  <i>“If you ever disappear on me, I would track you to the ends of the Earth and back. I will always find you, Bee. Always.”</i>
</b><br><br><i> From the author - Warning: This is not your typical romance. The story of Abby &amp; Jake contains disturbing situations, graphic violence, sex, strong language, drug use, and all types of abuse</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_766562550" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/766562550" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer766562550" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11524805063754115292"><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=4f9af628e40eaeb1eb0d4412c9c8a58d_zpsb01f72ef.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392817796i/8616257._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' height='400' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><b>Five Rip-Your-Heart-Out Torturously Dark Stars....</b><br/><br/><br/>This ain't your Momma's fluffy romance novels. If that's your cuppa, step away now. It. Was. Brutal. And I loved it! No judging me!<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&current=3765EB75-1AE5-423E-BE73-2B0F3C26C64E_zpssxloduhu.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392817796ra/8616258.gif' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' height='200' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>This is one of those books that I walk away from writing the review feeling like I didn't review it much at all because there's very little story I'm going to give away. It seriously needs to be experienced as it comes. But I'll try...<br/><br/><br/>One word to describe this book? DAMAGED. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=1088c517cbe3b8d45b7683f7e930b02e_zpsa4ae9358.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392817796i/8616259._SX540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Abby has a shit life. She's a 1</span>
  <span id="freeText11524805063754115292" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=4f9af628e40eaeb1eb0d4412c9c8a58d_zpsb01f72ef.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392817796i/8616257._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" height="400" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>Five Rip-Your-Heart-Out Torturously Dark Stars....</b><br><br><br>This ain't your Momma's fluffy romance novels. If that's your cuppa, step away now. It. Was. Brutal. And I loved it! No judging me!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=3765EB75-1AE5-423E-BE73-2B0F3C26C64E_zpssxloduhu.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392817796ra/8616258.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" height="200" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This is one of those books that I walk away from writing the review feeling like I didn't review it much at all because there's very little story I'm going to give away. It seriously needs to be experienced as it comes. But I'll try...<br><br><br>One word to describe this book? DAMAGED. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=1088c517cbe3b8d45b7683f7e930b02e_zpsa4ae9358.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392817796i/8616259._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Abby has a shit life. She's a 17-year old girl freshly graduated from high school. She has no friends to speak of and her parents are dead to her....DEAD. She has lived through trauma that no human being should endure. And now life deals her another blow. Her Nan, the one person on this earth she truly loves, dies and leaves her homeless and underage. She will NOT go back into the foster system. She'd rather go to prison....<br><br><br>Enter Jake. Ditto the Abby story. He's 22-years old and endured the loss of his mother and brother a few years ago. His dad hates him, wishes it was him who died that fateful day. He's been gone the past several years, never staying in one place for more than a few days, establishing no roots...and doing very illegal things. <br><br><br>When Jake and Abby meet, it's with the butt of his gun to her temple. She's trespassing on his dad's property...sleeping in an abandoned truck. But something just clicks for these two lost souls and their story begins....<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=b706f9187229adce56e813090748e39c_zps6dff21a1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392817796i/8616260._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Their story is raw. As I said, it's not for the light at heart. It's graphic...rape, assault, murder...you name it. Then add the heart strings they'll tug coupled with their experiences and it'll gut you. Consider this my last warning.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=4420F940-49F2-4034-B2D1-54DD67387A1F_zpsi4dn2jrr.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392817796ra/8616261.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I readily admit needing a bit of liquid courage to finish this story...<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=5D8A69F7-47E5-438B-8AED-A95E4044B1CA_zpsuknkdoef.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392817796ra/8616262.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>It's angsty but goes full circle. I was seriously praying for their semblance of a HEA. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Which you will get. In spades....I loved the ending. I had no clue how it would end up and it all wrapped up perfectly. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> So, if you're in the mood for something dark, raw, that'll tug on your heart, this book is for you. <br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=fbb53a7a62db9fe7d1bf2e68dabc0c34_zps66c50400.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392817796i/8616263._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Thank you...<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Blowing%20Kisses/?action=view&amp;current=C9AF9DC3-265C-403C-9CE1-61D97DB71E38_zpsymcoc5yp.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392678832ra/8593649.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gmka8yWOAhI5mcG2WPV2wRInmbwTcFKBw4FgkymRlGvGJfM1BBSIQM0giLCPmuURWWvU8qkr9lFmd133enFXrg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jSNUOrbXiu6eVWGMVT73P/V+C9466qMPBScXVUQJifXJb738l00AvGrsKIqCUWTvvjJGkICxB9+g0SoxF+lKMA==')})
  }

Unrivaled in both strength and social standing, Alik controls every facet of Kisa’s life, dominates her every move; keeps her subdued and dead inside...then one night changes everything. \n\nWhile working for her church—the only reprieve in her constant surveillance—Kisa stumbles across a tattooed, scarred, but stunningly beautiful homeless man on the streets. Something about him stirs feelings deep within her; familiar yet impossibly forbidden desires. He doesn’t talk. Doesn’t communicate with anyone. He’s a man beyond saving, and a man she must quickly forget...for both their sakes. \n\nBut when weeks later, out of the blue and to her complete surprise, he’s announced as the replacement fighter in The Dungeon, Kisa knows she’s in a whole lot of trouble. He’s built, ripped and lethally unforgiving to his opponents, leaving fear in his wake and the look of death in his eyes. \n\nKisa becomes obsessed with him. Yearns for him. Craves his touch. Needs to possess this mysterious man...this man they call Raze.\n\nDark Contemporary Romance. <span id="freeTextContainer16970802626624844059">T.M. (Tracey Marie) Frazier never dreamed that a single person would ever read a word she wrote when she published her first book. Now, she is a five-time USA Today bestselling author and her books have been translated into numerous languages and published all around the world. <br/><br/>T.M. enjoys writing what she calls ‘wrong side of the tracks romance’ with morally corrupt anti-heroes and ballsy heroine</span>
  <span id="freeText16970802626624844059" style="display:none">T.M. (Tracey Marie) Frazier never dreamed that a single person would ever read a word she wrote when she published her first book. Now, she is a five-time USA Today bestselling author and her books have been translated into numerous languages and published all around the world. <br /><br />T.M. enjoys writing what she calls ‘wrong side of the tracks romance’ with morally corrupt anti-heroes and ballsy heroines. <br /><br />Her books have been described as raw, dark and gritty. Basically, what that means, is while some authors are great at describing a flower as it blooms, T.M. is better at describing it in the final stages of decay. <br /><br />She loves meeting her readers, but if you see her at an event please don’t pinch her because she's not ready to wake up from this amazing dream. <br /><br />Join T.M. in Frazierland! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/tmfrazierland">www.facebook.com/groups/tmfrazierland</a></span>
